## 🤖 Instructions for LLM Processing

**Copy this entire document and paste it into Claude.ai or ChatGPT along with your existing achievement journal/brag document.**

### Suggested Prompt:

```
I have two documents:
1. My existing achievement journal (paste your current journal below)
2. Raw activity data from the past period (this document)

Please help me:
- Review the raw activities and identify significant accomplishments
- Group related activities into broader achievements
- Merge these new achievements into my existing journal
- Update any ongoing projects that have made progress
- Maintain chronological order and consistent formatting
- Highlight any particularly impressive or career-significant items

For each achievement, provide:
- Clear, results-oriented description
- Context about the impact or importance
- Relevant technical details or metrics
- Date or time period

Focus on accomplishments that would be relevant for:
- Performance reviews
- Resume updates
- Job interviews
- Promotion discussions
```

  in auth-client.ts. Previously was passing full endpoint URL which caused
  audience mismatch errors when calling user-profile-options endpoint.

  all service-to-service auth uses the correct base URL as the OIDC audience.

> [!NOTE]
> **Medium Risk**
> Changes the selection/classification rules and output schemas for scheduled BigQuery tables, which can materially shift who appears in recruiter queues and requires downstream consumers to handle new/renamed fields.
> 
> **Overview**
> Updates Priority View’s BigQuery pipelines to broaden role coverage and make candidate outreach targeting more precise.
> 
> `priority_view_role_stats` now includes **all active opportunities** (not just focus-area matches) and adds an `is_focus_area` boolean to let downstream services prioritize focus roles while still showing other roles.
> 
> `priority_view_candidates` expands contact classification to include `favorable_history` and tightens `needs_bump` logic (7–30 day outbound window, excludes candidates who applied after being marked Engaged/Interested). It also adds funnel-mapped application context (via `application_status_funnel_mappings` and `qualified_application_details`), enforces a 12-month recency window for `favorable_history`, and outputs additional columns (last inbound/outbound timestamps and last application details). Documentation in `README.md` is updated to reflect the new definitions, schemas, clustering, and service query pattern.
>

#### #1048: More carefully merge edu history - ✅ merged ([link](https://github.com/WorkUp-Health/WorkUp-Service/pull/1048))

- **Changes:** 2 files (+164 / -28)
- **Created:** Jan 20, 2026
- **Merged:** Jan 20, 2026

**Description:**
https://app.frontapp.com/inboxes/teammates/24942428/inbox/open/118903006620

Doesn't need to be a hotfix - this is just an improvement on checking for duplicate education records. The user was imported like 10 times in 10 minutes with unclear education levels so we kept inserting new records.

<!-- CURSOR_SUMMARY -->
---

> [!NOTE]
> Refines education history merging to reduce duplicate records and normalize data.
> 
> - Match on `school_id`/`other_school_name` plus `graduation_date` (not `level_of_education`), with ordered selection for stability
> - Treat empty/whitespace `levelOfEducation` as null; trim values before storing updates
> - If both records have `levelOfEducation` and they differ, insert a new record; otherwise merge and fill `level_of_education`, `area_of_study`, and `graduation_month`
> - Skip dedup only when `graduation_date` is missing; still attempt when `levelOfEducation` is missing
> - SQL updated to fetch `level_of_education` and use `TRIM()` comparisons; update allowlist expanded
> - Comprehensive tests updated/added to cover matching, merging, trimming, and differing degree scenarios
> 
> <sup>Written by [Cursor Bugbot](https://cursor.com/dashboard?tab=bugbot) for commit dd9ec74e0240926411a68bf24951446f933c1fea. This will update automatically on new commits. Configure [here](https://cursor.com/dashboard?tab=bugbot).</sup>
<!-- /CURSOR_SUMMARY -->

#### #1038: HOTFIX: Update merging user data to not stop on FK violations - ✅ merged ([link](https://github.com/WorkUp-Health/WorkUp-Service/pull/1038))

- **Changes:** 1 files (+130 / -67)
- **Created:** Jan 12, 2026
- **Merged:** Jan 12, 2026

**Description:**
When we're getting those Foreign Key violation warnings (when Gemini hallucinates role or specialty IDs) that user merge/save process just exits, so anything after that is not getting saved to postgres. I'm wrapping them in try-catches here so one failure isn't cascading and we still save the other data after an FK violation.

I'm going to try to tweak the prompt too (even though it already tells Gemini to use the role and specialties lists and validate against them 🤷‍♂️ 🤖 )

https://app.frontapp.com/open/cnv_1ikwx4t8?key=SNwi3FIoEEOKY2w0XUJrc_lvalOXiX62

<!-- CURSOR_SUMMARY -->
---

> [!NOTE]
> Improves resilience of user import/merge by isolating failures and continuing processing.
> 
> - Wraps saves in `try/catch` with `logger.warn` and continues on error: `saveUserWorkHistory`, `saveUserEducation`, `saveUserCareerPreferences` (roles, specialties, levels), `saveUserAddress`, and license merges
> - Enhances address handling: only insert if none exists, resolve location ID, log when unresolved, and catch general save errors
> - Notes sequential processing still used; each section now handles its own errors to avoid blocking others
>

#### Re-introduce fallback location for candidates in rediscovery ([link](https://app.clickup.com/t/86add3ka5))

- **Folder:** Product
- **List:** Delivery
- **Created:** Nov 20, 2025
- **Updated:** Nov 28, 2025
- **Closed:** Nov 21, 2025

Background
Given we leverage location of most recent app as a fallback for candidates when they don't have one set, we want to re-introduce that to the rediscovery UI (and maybe more generally) but give it a visual treatemtn like the attached design that flags that to the user. The belief is users may see that once, understand it and move on, so we don't want it to overwhelm the UI.

Acceptance Criteria
Given I am a user reviewing candidates
When a candidate doesn't have a location set on their profile but they do have application history
Then I should see their location displayed based on their most recent app with an info icon as designed
And When I hover on the icon
Then I should see text that says "Candidate location unavailable; defaulting to the facility location of their last application."

Design (feel free to wrap text)

#### Backfill email/SMS sources to be not system-specific ([link](https://app.clickup.com/t/86acvqd82))

- **Folder:** Product
- **List:** Delivery

- **Updated:** Nov 20, 2025
- **Closed:** Nov 20, 2025

**Background**
Currently, in the admin app candidate drawer, we display the details of a candidates' Email/SMS activity for super admins only. 
For "regular" admin app users, we do not display any additional data beyond the event type (Ex. "Email sent", "Email opened", etc.) since some of the email titles have system-specific information. 

We want to backfill these email and sms activity source s (the column where the email title is stored) so that these titles are not specific to a system and we can display these to all users. 

This will require us to backfill via Segment, so that Segment writes these updated titles to their respective BQ tables.

Users who are associated with an email title in t he above list in any of their email/sms activity, should have their Segment events related to these email/sms activities backfilled.

Previous Segment backfills

#### [Matching] Adjust location handling ([link](https://app.clickup.com/t/86ackdecx))

- **Folder:** Product
- **List:** Delivery
- **Created:** Oct 16, 2025
- **Updated:** Nov 21, 2025
- **Closed:** Oct 23, 2025

Match score incorporates candidate location by check either the location set on a candidate or falling back to see if a candidate recently applied to a role (application history) and using the location as a proxy. In the match results, we show the location of the candidates even if we used the fallback value from application history. This is somewhat confusing because when you click to see the candidate detail, their locations are often blank.
Example
Go to  
See that "Aminah Kaba" has a location listed in the table
Click on candidate
See that they do not have a location listed in the drawer (their application history does have a recent application in the location listed in the table)

Suggested change
Only show location in the match if we have a candidate.location (not exact field name), otherwise, keep it blank.
ALT: italicize the proxied location and/or add small subtext that says "taken from/based on recent application"
Ensure the candidate summary incorporates a sentence explaining that the recent application was used as a proxy to match them - "Previously applied to a role in Morristown, NJ."

#### write logic to calculate overall match score, warmth score and location score ([link](https://app.clickup.com/t/86acc3q1f))

- **Folder:** Sprints
- **List:** Sprint 20 (10/5 - 10/18)
- **Created:** Oct 7, 2025
- **Updated:** Oct 15, 2025
- **Closed:** Oct 15, 2025

"Matching"
role match - define what fields from opp we can query for in users table (e.g. careerRole)
opp.careerRole  = userPreferences.role
opp.careerRole = workHistory.roleId
application joined with opp.careerRole = workhistory.roleid or userpreferences.role
past-applicant-data.processed.workup_user_applications_latest_status 
location match - opp location matched to user location, if no user location, check if recent applications have location and use as proxy
PRIMARY: user.current_location_id and/or useraddress.location_id = opp.location_id(s) (not actually equal but instead proximity based)
FALLBACK: most recent application joined with opp.location_ids = opp.location_id 
<= 5 miles = 4 points
5-10 miles = 3
10-20 = 2
>20 = 1
warmth - positive engagement
<=15 days = 4
15 - 30 = 3
30 - 90 = 2
>90 = 1
no engagement = 0
Activities included:
email/sms click/reply
opp apply button click
viewed opp/any app engagement
applied to job
 
Columns
user_id
opp_id (location, career role)
overall match_score
location_score
engagement_score
 
When a user is updated or an opp is created, setup new rows - overkill?
 
get role matches and create table with user_id, opp_id
query for unique user locations,

#### User reviewing events should see hyperlinked registrant # ([link](https://app.clickup.com/t/86advjfdy))

- **Folder:** Sprints
- **List:** Sprint 25 (12/14 - 12/27)
- **Created:** Dec 10, 2025
- **Updated:** Dec 18, 2025
- **Closed:** Dec 18, 2025

Background
It seems like a lot of our users are trying to access the info on candidates signing up for events and our UX isn't clear on how to get there. What we want to do in future iterations and what would make the most sense is to hyperlink the # shown for registrants/sign up and when a user clicks that they get taken to the events view with a filtered view of candidates.

Acceptance Criteria
Given I am a user looking at the events table (on the events page or dashboard)
When I see an event with >0 sign ups
Then I should see that number hyperlinked
...
And When I click that number
Then I should be taken to the events page with a filtered view of candidates that signed up for that events

#### Bugfixes for New Apply Flow for Metlife - Work History ([link](https://app.clickup.com/t/86aej6un2))

- **Folder:** Sprints
- **List:** Sprint 27 (1/11 - 1/24)
- **Tags:** bug
- **Created:** Jan 15, 2026
- **Updated:** Jan 15, 2026
- **Closed:** Jan 15, 2026

I put in a hotfix here:  

But we'll need to follow up with how to fix this more long term (i.e. remove from registration flow and keep in apply flow? Or opposite?). Either way the work history needs to be merged, not duplicated or deleted and overwritten. 

Pre-hotfix: a user would fill out work history and we would send two save requests for work history around the same time - creating two nearly duplicate rows in user_work_history  in postgres and displaying in our frontends. The mergeWorkHistory() function actually pulls in all of the correct ids (like roleId) and the saveUserAnswers()  does not

#### Add the ability to capture walk-ins/add candidates to events ([link](https://app.clickup.com/t/86aejarv4))

- **Folder:** Sprints
- **List:** Sprint 28 (1/25 - 2/7)
- **Created:** Jan 15, 2026
- **Updated:** Feb 5, 2026
- **Closed:** Feb 5, 2026

Background
For events, especially those with pre-registration like MetLife, AHS/customers often have walk-ins or people that show up. As a result, we want to make sure we give them the ability to add candidates.

Acceptance Criteria
With this task, users should:
Show a button in the top right corner of an event to "Add Candidate"
When a user clicks that button, a pop-up is shown to enter their email address
When a user "searches" for that email address, we either display their info pre-populated or don't (see screenshots)
When a user is completing their info, they should have the option to mark them as attended (default to checked)
When submitting, this candidate should be displayed in the table as a full registrant

Designs
See attached or prototype here - meant to be illustrative

#### Improve our matching of candidates as fits for roles ([link](https://app.clickup.com/t/86af6a18f))

- **Folder:** Sprints
- **List:** Sprint 30 (2/22 - 3/7)
- **Created:** Feb 7, 2026
- **Updated:** Feb 24, 2026

Acceptance Criteria
Scenarios where we are currently seeing candidates being matched to roles that aren't good fits:

BB Notes for what was done:
  Scoring improvements (BQ SQL):
  - 8-bucket location scoring (was 4 coarse buckets) — better differentiation within 25mi
  - 8-bucket warmth float (was 4 integer) — splits the 72% mega-bucket by recency
  - Rejection penalty based on rate/count (-0.25/-0.15/-0.10)
  - Overall score formula rewrite for the buckets above with 0.6-10.0 clamping
  - Specialty matching bonus (+0.5 when candidate specialty matches opportunity)
  - 44 new career role aliases for better Tier 4 role inference

  Structural fixes (BQ SQL):
  - First-label role inference replacing CROSS JOIN UNNEST (fixes multi-label contamination for 41.7K users)
  - Rejection + specialty folded into qualifications term for proper weighting
  - Last-application tiebreaker, specialty case sensitivity, specialty_id FK

  UI/Service fixes:
  - Fixed sorting bug causing 419K rows to sort as lowest-priority (Service)
  - Added candidateStatus filter (is/is not) to Rediscovery and Candidates pages
  - Default Rediscovery filters: exclude Not Interested + Took Role Elsewhere
  - Aligned Priority View filters with FilterSummaryCard system (6.3 "Good" threshold)

  Data fixes:
  - 117 disqualification patterns (was 81) — 3 rounds of additions + FP audit
  - SMS STOP reply filtering from engagement scores
  - IR Technologist career role created + 29 opps reprocessed
  - Career preferences set for 6 complaint candidates
  - 4 Radiology Assistant opps reclassified (were mislabeled as Rad Tech)
  - Bulk reprocessing: all active opps (3 systems) + 11,337 inactive AHS opps

  Complaint resolution: 27/34 named candidates resolved (79%). Remaining 5 are internal employee detection (deferred to product scoping) + 2 partial improvements.
